It can be seen that the hotel staff are carefully selected.
Usually when I stay in a hotel, I rarely write a review, but the staff here are really great. There is a sister Zou Huaiqin at the front desk who is really attentive to details.
First of all, he is very approachable and his speaking voice is really comfortable. I wonder if this is also specially trained. I asked her where the bathroom in the lobby was. Unlike other hotel staff, she just gave you a general indication and was done. She also took me there specifically to the bathroom door. When I was at the front desk, I casually asked if there were less crowded tourist attractions in Chengdu that were worth visiting. When I went downstairs after putting my luggage away, she ran over to show me several places worth visiting and asked me If you like that type of attraction, tell me the route and tell me what I need to pay attention to.
After I came back from playing, he asked me how I felt. He told me that if I wanted to take a walk in the evening, I could go to Sichuan University and recommended a super delicious fried potato shop.
To be honest, it's beyond my expectation that a hotel staff can be so detailed and attentive. She said that their hotel's philosophy is to treat guests as family members, and they really did it.
If you come to Chengdu next time, you will definitely come here. I will also recommend friends and colleagues to experience it here. I will give you 10,000 likes!

Next to Jiuyan Bridge, it is within ten minutes of shared bicycles. Since it is near the university, Kaifeng cuisine, Golden Arch Gate, Ruixing, etc. are all available in Moziqiao area. At the same time, there are more restaurants in Jiuyanqiao Bar Street, which can be a better alternative to going to Chunxi Road to join in the fun. s Choice;
3. Service. The implementation of the butler system in hotels is not new, but it was an experience a long time ago. The hotel has a guest relations team that takes the initiative to contact and communicate after the order is completed, paying attention to the relevant requirements and details of the guests. This is not easy for a large-scale hotel, after all, there are few staff during the Spring Festival and The inverse ratio to the large number of customers, especially the patience with a talkative customer, is worthy of praise. The entire hotel, from welcoming guests to cleaning, greets guests warmly when they see them, which also reflects the overall level and corporate culture of the hotel. On the day I left the hotel, I saw someone wearing Hanfu doing a live broadcast in the hotel. If I wasn‚Äôt in a hurry to catch a flight, I would have really wanted to listen to it;
4. Facilities. Originally, I planned to walk around the hotel to see what the pavilions and pavilions in the promotion were like, but unfortunately I went out late every night and came back late every day, so it didn't happen. The facilities in the room are good, but I didn't get to experience the facilities in the hotel because I went out late and came back late.
Overall evaluation: 2024 is the first Spring Festival period without the impact of the epidemic in the post-epidemic era. Going to Wuhou Temple and Kuanzhai Alley has fully realized the power of its crowds. Against this backdrop, being able to stay in a five-star hotel with cost-effective price, convenient transportation, and good overall reviews, and being able to retreat and rest quietly after a day of running around in the hustle and bustle, should be one of the highlights of this short trip. The most correct choice.
